  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_029b3591-1cc8-4878-8997-a23c5f54744e'
      });

  <span id="freeText4948796795797137652" style="display:none">Lauren Brooks fell in love with Cal Scott at 21, married him at 22 and had her heart broken at 23 when he walked out of their marriage. At 25, though raising his daughter on her own, Lauren was finally moving on with her life. Until, she learned the reason for Cal's abandonment, the walls she’d carefully built around her collapsed..<br /> <br />The day she meets Chris, all those feelings she thought she had bottled up come spilling out. She can’t afford to give into her heart’s desire again. Love nearly broke her once, and her daughter doesn't need two broken parents.<br /><br />Christopher Scott is in love, newly engaged to Jenna, who saw him through an illness he didn’t think he could survive. He’s finally settling into the life he’s always wanted, making plans he only dared to dream before now.<br /><br />Until, a woman named Lauren arrives on his doorstep.<br /><br />She’s intriguing, beautiful and, try as he might, he can’t stay away. The closer he gets to her, the more his rock-solid plans begin to crumble. All he knows is that Lauren is the missing piece to a puzzle he must solve. For him to put all the pieces in place, he’ll have to follow his heart, and that might cost him everything...</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1044175655" />
    <a title="Maria " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5769334-maria"><img alt="Maria " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600318539p2/5769334.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1044175655?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria " href="/user/show/5769334-maria">Maria </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1044175655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10828413796394967024"><b>
  <u>REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</u>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416636879ra/12024117.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>That fucking cliffhanger!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416636879ra/12024118.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Seriously?!</b><br/><i>It has to end on the part where things are starting to get really, really good!!!</i><br/><br/>Then we'll have to wait again to see what happens to this twisted love square. <br/><br/><b>So freakin' evil Portia!</b> So freakin' evil.<br/><br/>First of all, I just want to say that I really enjoyed this book. There were times that I got annoyed because the Lauren became a tiny bit annoying. There were times when she didn't seem like the same girl I liked from the fir</span>
  <span id="freeText10828413796394967024" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416636879ra/12024117.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>That fucking cliffhanger!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416636879ra/12024118.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Seriously?!</b><br><i>It has to end on the part where things are starting to get really, really good!!!</i><br><br>Then we'll have to wait again to see what happens to this twisted love square. <br><br><b>So freakin' evil Portia!</b> So freakin' evil.<br><br>First of all, I just want to say that I really enjoyed this book. There were times that I got annoyed because the Lauren became a tiny bit annoying. There were times when she didn't seem like the same girl I liked from the first book.<br><br><b>Still, I loved this book!</b><br><br><i>The cover. Can I just emphasize how much I love that cover.<br>The twists.<br>The characters.<br>The writing.<br>The pace.</i><br><b>I really loved it!</b><br><br><b>
  <u>HOW IT STARTS</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>How the fuck did I end up here? It's the same question I've asked myself a thousand times.</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>THE GIST<u></u></u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Everything is great, except I'm in love with a man who really has no idea who I am and he's engaged to be married to another woman. Other than that, things are dandy.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Lauren still could not believe how complicated life had been for her after loving Cal. After disappearing on her a few years after they got married, she soon realised why Cal left. <b>But that didn't make things easier for her and Caylen.</b> In fact, it made things even more complicated.<br><br>Not only does she have to deal with Cal's parents <s>his dad was absolutely insufferable!</s>,but she also had to deal with another woman. <br><br><i>I'm not going to give anything away more on here as it will be a huge spoiler for the first book.</i> So sorry. But this is as much summary as I could give you. ^_^<br><br><b>
  <u>MY INITIAL REACTIONS<u></u></u>
</b><br><br>I really liked the first book and the novella. I felt really connected to all of the characters even the secondary ones. I've always loved books that make me curious, and the first book <i>If I Break</i> definitely did that for me. <br><br>So when Portia offered me to read and review the ARC version of this book, why the fuck would I say no? <br><br><b>The first few pages was enough to stir up my emotions.</b> That was how good it was for me.<br><br><b>
  <u>MEET THE CHARACTERS<u></u></u>
</b><br><br><b>Lauren:</b> I didn't particularly like Lauren here, especially during the middle to the end of the book. She became a bit too obsessed with Chris. I felt that Cal's dad was right and that she was forgetting who Chris and Cal really is.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>It's very wrong that his texts are something I look forward to now. It's been two weeks since we were with him. He sends them in the morning and usually around four. We started skyping after I got back home.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I get where the problem is though. Chris reminds her of Cal, but they are different. <b>Same but different.</b> And as much as I would like to blurt it out here what the stupid difference is... I can't.. I don't want to spoil anyone. Soooo... <br><br>Going back to Lauren, some of her decisions have been rash and inconsiderate to the people around her like her friends and Raven. <b>Her reason was because it was for Caylen, which I totally do NOT agree at all.</b> She didn't do it for Caylen, she did some of the things she did for herself, to fill that void she was feeling when she lost Cal. <i>But did she really lose Cal?</i><br><br><b>Chris:</b> I absolutely feel bad for this guy. I feel that he is caught in the middle of something he can control and something he couldn't. <b>But there is a part of me that hates him because he's being a fucking pussy!</b> <i>If you're not sure about how you feel about someone, let them fucking know!</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Every determination I have is being employed to stamp out every urge to wrap my arms around the small of her back, pulling her against me and kissing her lips that are barely open but begging me to taste them.<br><br>This isn't good.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>That definitely isn't good Chris, but I don't blame you.</b> Just stop being a whimp and you'll be fine.<br><br><b>Cal:</b> I really missed Cal. You don't get to see much of him here, but you'll know he's there, lurking beneath the shadows of everything. <b>Before you ask, I just want to say that, No, Cal isn't dead.</b> Hehe<br><br><b>The Secondary Characters:</b> I want to say that I hate Cal's dad with some much passion, I want to push him in front of a freakin truck. Oh and not only that, I hate Jenna too. What a fucking stuck-up bitch. Seriously. Cal's Dad and Jenna should be together. I think they're made for each other.<br><br>I don't hate all the secondary characters, I do love Chris' friends: Aidan and Lisa. Also, Chris' mom isn't too bad. i actually kind of liked her. <br><br><b>
  <u>THE ROMANCE</u>
</b><br><br>I'm a bit torned apart here. I'm not sure who I like more for Lauren, Chris or Cal. Yeah, I'm not entirely sure who she should end up with because both guys have their own strengths you know.<br><br>While Cal is a cocky, son-of-a-bitch, he genuinely loved Lauren, and I'm sure Caylen too. And Chris should know that. He saw it. Hehe. Not gonna say how. LOL. But he was also a bit, secretive and distant at times, which makes Lauren really upset. But now that his secret his out, if he does come back, I'm sure Lauren would still want him. <b>But what about Chris?</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>As wild and unpredictable as Cal was, I knew Cal. At least I thought I did. I was comfortable in the whirlwind that was our life together. Chris is a totally different story. Falling for him is dangerous, and pursuing him comes with a whole lot of risk.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Be ready for a whole lot of <b>sexual tension</b> in this book.<br><br>I feel the connection between Lauren and Chris, they are more alike that Lauren and Cal. But I still believe that Lauren should be with Cal... even though... yeah forget it... if you guys have read this and want to discuss this mindfucking situation, please message me. I do want to talk to someone about this.<br><br><b>
  <u>FINAL RAMBLINGS</u>
</b><br><br><b>The Writing:</b> I writing is still as good as the first one for me. I feel connected and emotionally attached to the situation and the character so that must be saying something. <br><br><b>The Good Stuff:</b><br><br>1. The plot twists. I just love how Portia always seems to suprise me!! The ending. The epicness of it was just... Too much to handle.<br><br>2. The character development was pretty evident as well. How Chris' and the people around his life got affected by Lauren and Caylen's arrival. The reaction of the involved characters were very realistic.<br><br>3. The ending! Oh holy hell.<br><br><b>The Not-So-Good-Stuff:</b><br><br>1. I didn't like Lauren slowly warming up to Chris. I just don't like it. I love Cal, maybe it's wrong to like him for Lauren because he's unstable, but... yeah... <b>TEAM CAL!</b><br><br>2. Lauren. Hehe. Stupid hormones.<br><br><b>LAST WORDS:</b> I really liked this series and it really glued me to the edge of my seat as did the last book and its novella. I feel that there's something about the story that I just couldn't help but be drawn to.<br><br>Of course, it does have its shortcomings, but it didn't really matter to me. <b>And I suppose a book doesn't necessarily have to be perfect for it to be enjoyable.</b> And this book was that for me.<br><br>I would recommend this book to anyone who would be interesting in a mindfucking contemporary book, that would keep you glued up until the last page.<br><br>Last but not the least, <b>I would like to thank Portia Moore for providing me with this ARC copy for review.</b> I really, really, really enjoyed Lauren, Cal, and Chris story. I'll be patiently waiting for the next book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10828413796394967024" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3146962344" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2664296316153385265"><i>
  <b>3.5 stars</b>
</i><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝ In the end, we’re all searching for what will make us sleep well at night, give us peace even when everything isn’t perfect. ❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Okay, so I'm kind of confused on what books I read because one of them was only in male pov, and then it ended and another one started which also said it was the second book? It continued off where the last "book" and/or "part" ended so I'm just rating them as a whole because the ebooks weren't formatted in the best way so I'm not really sure if</span>
  <span id="freeText2664296316153385265" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>3.5 stars</b>
</i><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝ In the end, we’re all searching for what will make us sleep well at night, give us peace even when everything isn’t perfect. ❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Okay, so I'm kind of confused on what books I read because one of them was only in male pov, and then it ended and another one started which also said it was the second book? It continued off where the last "book" and/or "part" ended so I'm just rating them as a whole because the ebooks weren't formatted in the best way so I'm not really sure if one of them was an extra story or not.<br /><br />First off, the thing I like about this series is that it's very engaging. I don't want to spoil anything, but this just isn't a typical love story where there's one conflict and it's easily solved in the end. This shows real issues in our society today and it's a really raw book in the sense that it shows a deep dive into life. Life is messy, full of drama, and complicated. This shows that, and doesn't sugar coat it. <br /><br />I actually liked Lauren as a character and enjoyed her povs most. I loved how she put her daughter before anything, and was brave even when she wanted to break down. I actually thought the writing for the male pov was done right. The author really captured the character's essence, and I could've easily guessed whose who without any disclaimer. <br /><br />I gave this book 3.5 stars because it really did capture my attention, and I'm currently binge reading the entire series which is always a good sign. I enjoyed it more than the first. The writing is simple and flows well, there were some spelling mistakes, but I feel like in most ebooks I've read there are so I'm not going to go in depth with that.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the fresh take this had on a contemporary romance novel. If I'm being honest, I usually always have something to complain about, but I think this was actually a great way to pass the time (and procrastinate studying).<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/rayne.reads/" rel="nofollow noopener">instagram</a> <b>|</b> <a href="https://havenofink.home.blog" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a> <b>| </b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/102337987-rayne/" rel="nofollow noopener">goodreads</a></span>

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3135809657" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4114705756294506696">Fuck, this series is good! 😍 At this point, telling what the story is about would spoil it. I'm having such a great time reading it though! I'm actually shocked at how much I'm enjoying it!<br/><br/>That's why I love getting recommendations of older books. You find hidden gems. I have never heard of this series or this author in my life until my friend recommended it to me the other day when I asked a question on social media about a book or series that consumed you. Shout out to Courtney for this amazing</span>
  <span id="freeText4114705756294506696" style="display:none">Fuck, this series is good! 😍 At this point, telling what the story is about would spoil it. I'm having such a great time reading it though! I'm actually shocked at how much I'm enjoying it!<br /><br />That's why I love getting recommendations of older books. You find hidden gems. I have never heard of this series or this author in my life until my friend recommended it to me the other day when I asked a question on social media about a book or series that consumed you. Shout out to Courtney for this amazing recommendation! 🤩</span>
  <a data-text-id="4114705756294506696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1039056852" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1039056852" />
    <a title="Nawal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31586926-nawal"><img alt="Nawal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450820120p2/31586926.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1039056852?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nawal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nawal" href="/user/show/31586926-nawal">Nawal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31586926-nawal?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31586926-nawal?shelf=drama">drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1039056852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4647454703844852810"><b>Please note: Before reading this, I recommend reading the first part ‘If I Break’ . It is currently FREE on Amazon so I really hope you take a chance on it!</b><br/><br/>What a wonderful sequel! This book had me in love from beginning to end.<br/><br/>The storyline: Lauren finally discovers Cal’s secret only to be led to even more confusion. Things aren’t looking like they’ll be getting any better but she does what she must do to keep her daughter Caylen out of this tragedy and have a loving family around her. Lauren h</span>
  <span id="freeText4647454703844852810" style="display:none"><b>Please note: Before reading this, I recommend reading the first part ‘If I Break’ . It is currently FREE on Amazon so I really hope you take a chance on it!</b><br /><br />What a wonderful sequel! This book had me in love from beginning to end.<br /><br />The storyline: Lauren finally discovers Cal’s secret only to be led to even more confusion. Things aren’t looking like they’ll be getting any better but she does what she must do to keep her daughter Caylen out of this tragedy and have a loving family around her. Lauren has to forget about what she wants and keep her focus around her child. With Chris in the picture, things may not go according to plan. And Chris senses it too. With living a happy life with his fiancée, he sees the trouble Lauren could bring and shake the balance of his world.<br /><br />This book was as good as I had anticipated. I may have even liked it better than its first part although I must confess I missed Cal terribly. In the first book we see Cal and his ‘I don’t give a shit’ attitude which explains my liking to him so much while contrastingly, Chris is one of the nicest guys you could probably meet. They were both such great characters to have had an opportunity to read about and I enjoyed the perspectives alternating in this book between Lauren and Chris.<br /><br />One of my most favourite parts about this book was Lauren’s tribulations. Call me depressing but I just connected with her so much. Her character was well bought out, her suffering undeniable. But she survived. She fought. She accepted. And I loved her. The way it was written bought to life everything she was going through because I don’t think anyone can go through what she did and come out whole. Sorry but I just feel so strongly about her story. She didn’t succumb to the pain but she did what had to be done, all for her daughter. Hats off to her for becoming one of my favourite book heroines.<br /><br />Chris’ development was also something I enjoyed reading about. That man has serious issues. I felt sorry for him mostly but there were times when I felt bad for Lauren, due to his actions. He had many qualities though. He was just so nice, the complete opposite of what Lauren is used to but he may just be that chance at love Lauren needs again. He’s caught up between two women, not knowing which direction to take, what’s real and what isn’t. His life is more than a little confusing.<br /><br />I honestly have nothing negative to say about this book. It delivered what I expected it to and I enjoyed the readers experience from beginning to end. I adored the characterisation, and the story…well let’s just say that was my favourite part. It was special, a little different and it’s one of those where you just cannot wait to find out what happens next. I will be waiting eagerly for spring 2015, bring on book 3! I recommend this to all romance lovers. Especially those who like a little anticipation and a storyline that keeps you wanting to know what happens next.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>my eyes drift over to Chris. I’ve been trying to avoid looking at him. I haven’t been here that long, but I told myself that I shouldn’t look at him for more than five seconds. My eyes didn’t agree with me earlier. They still don’t seem to now. They follow his every move, waiting for another glimpse of who I saw earlier.</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4647454703844852810" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15761145700933500679"><b>Advance Readers Copy (ARC) provided for my blog for an honest review by the lovely author Portia Moore<br/><br/>Title: Almost Broken<br/>Series: If I Break, #2<br/>Author: Portia Moore<br/>Release Date: November 14th, 2014<br/>Rating: 5 Stars<br/>Cliffhanger: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/>HEA: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Not Exactly <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><u>Character Casting:</u><br/><br/>Lauren - <br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=1ou5gh' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415529911i/11806322._SY540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Chris/Cal - <br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2qurq5y' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415531337i/11806523._SY540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a></b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>Review:</b>
</u><br/>This book was thrilling, amazing on the 'end of your seat' series that you just wish the heroine will get her happy ending. I was honored to be </span>
  <span id="freeText15761145700933500679" style="display:none"><b>Advance Readers Copy (ARC) provided for my blog for an honest review by the lovely author Portia Moore<br><br>Title: Almost Broken<br>Series: If I Break, #2<br>Author: Portia Moore<br>Release Date: November 14th, 2014<br>Rating: 5 Stars<br>Cliffhanger: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>HEA: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not Exactly <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><u>Character Casting:</u><br><br>Lauren - <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=1ou5gh" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415529911i/11806322._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Chris/Cal - <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2qurq5y" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415531337i/11806523._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b><br><br><u>
  <b>Review:</b>
</u><br>This book was thrilling, amazing on the 'end of your seat' series that you just wish the heroine will get her happy ending. I was honored to be given an ARC of this series and I can't explain in words how much I loved it. It does go a bit slow in the beginning but makes it up in the middle and the end of the book with a twist you never saw coming. <br><br><b>Is Cal really gone? I'm not going to answer that, you have to find out on your own</b>.<br><br>Portia Moore made an interesting book original, we get dual POV which is amazing because we get to find out what is going on in both their heads. But when I say you'll going to hate Mr.Scott &amp; Jenna they will make you want to smack them more than twice.<br><br>Even though we get more answers they're so much more unanswered. I seriously can't wait for the final book. because this book just left me hanging on a thread and I need more. <br><br>My Review of If I Break ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tinyurl.com/q4kcpq9">http://tinyurl.com/q4kcpq9</a><br>My Review of Before I Break ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tinyurl.com/mnekzyo">http://tinyurl.com/mnekzyo</a><br><br><b><u>Follow Me:</u><br>Twitter:</b> @BeyondBReviews<br><b>Pinterest:</b> @Beyondboyfriend<br><b>Facebook:</b> /Beyondboyfriendreviews<br><b>Blog:</b> Beyondboyfriendreviews.tumblr.com<br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1005075165" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1005075165" />
    <a title="Christine Alibutud" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21902672-christine-alibutud"><img alt="Christine Alibutud" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464518292p2/21902672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1005075165?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Alibutud" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Alibutud" href="/user/show/21902672-christine-alibutud">Christine Alibutud</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1005075165" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer872231941344692193"><i>Note: I received an ARC from the author in exchange for a review.</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The thing is I think I am broken, almost at least."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418030626ra/12647590.gif' width='350' height='225' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Just when I thought I've had enough cliffhangers with this series...Yep, couldn't have been more wrong! <b>BUT!</b> This installment was just what I needed after that very long and depressing reading hiatus I had for almost two months now. I've been quite busy with my academics and I really haven't found time to squeeze in a little good reading and do some book reviews---bot</span>
  <span id="freeText872231941344692193" style="display:none"><i>Note: I received an ARC from the author in exchange for a review.</i><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The thing is I think I am broken, almost at least."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418030626ra/12647590.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just when I thought I've had enough cliffhangers with this series...Yep, couldn't have been more wrong! <b>BUT!</b> This installment was just what I needed after that very long and depressing reading hiatus I had for almost two months now. I've been quite busy with my academics and I really haven't found time to squeeze in a little good reading and do some book reviews---both of which I absolutely missed. So, I am very sorry Ms. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8224620.Portia_Moore" title="Portia Moore" rel="nofollow noopener">Portia Moore</a> for not doing my book review as soon as you gave me an ARC of this. There was just so many things going on and I really couldn't find time to read this, even though it was all I wanted to do. Thank heavens that I finally did read this, and it definitely was the right cure to my reading hiatus.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Everything is great, except I’m in love with a man who really has no idea who I am and he’s engaged to be married to another woman."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418028244ra/12647096.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22364538.If_I_Break" title="If I Break by Portia Moore" rel="nofollow noopener">If I Break</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23205189.Before_I_Break__If_I_Break_1_5_" title="Before I Break (If I Break 1.5) by Portia Moore" rel="nofollow noopener">Before I Break</a>, both of which ended with a very devastating and nail-biting cliffhanger, I wanted to get my hands as soon as possible with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23574818.Almost_Broken__If_I_Break__2_" title="Almost Broken (If I Break #2) by Portia Moore" rel="nofollow noopener">Almost Broken</a>. The first two installments got me depressed for days, and safe to say, this recent book also ended with a good book hangover. <br><i>
  <blockquote>"If he could just remember something about us, about me, our life together. It’s pathetic. I know, but it would make me feel some consolation. If Cal loved me and he’s a part of him, he should feel something. Even if it’s locked away in another part of his mind, he should remember something."</blockquote>
</i> <br>I have really grown to empathize with Lauren all throughout. With everything that has happened to her, which shattered everything she thought she knew and caused a major change in her life, you can see that she has a strong personality, but is actually a fragile person deep inside.<br><i>
  <blockquote>"She’s strong, but fragile. She puts up a hard shell around herself but she’s vulnerable, and I know my actions affect her more than anyone, well almost anyone, and that’s the problem."</blockquote>
</i><br>In connection with Lauren's vulnerability, this then brings me to Chris. Okay, first thing's first, I love Chris---just as much as I love Cal. When I compare the two, they are entirely different, but somehow, pretty much the same. Although I did fall in love with Cal first, I have grown an attachment to Chris. I guess, in a way, I can feel what Lauren is feeling. It's easy to distinguish Chris from Cal, but at the same time, so hard to separate the two personalities. <br><i>
  <blockquote>"His eyes lock into mine, and for a second, he looks at me how Cal used to, with an intensity that overwhelmed me, that used to consume me."</blockquote>
</i> <br>Chris' DID is definitely a difficult case to handle, and his disorder managed to completely mess numerous lives, especially Lauren's, his very own, and even Jenna's. Also, can I just say that as much as I want to feel bad for Jenna and understand what she's going through, I absolutely despise her. She's not making it easier for anyone. In addition to this, let me bring up Chris' dad as well. I don't like how he's so cold to Lauren, and is most of the time, rude to her. <br><br>I'm just like<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401503806ra/9812464.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, Chris' mom, his friends, Lisa and Aidan, Raven, and Caylen also added nice touches to this book. I love their characters, and I really liked how they played important parts to the lives of Chris and Lauren.<br><br>But of course, I can't help but really feel bad whenever Lauren and Chris suppress their feelings for each other.<br><i>
  <blockquote>"It’s a lot harder than I thought it’d be, pretending to be indifferent and not in love with a person sitting a few inches from you and even harder when you see firsthand they love someone else."</blockquote>
</i><br>At least Lauren was aware of her feelings, and accepted it to herself, but Chris continued being stubborn. <br><br>But until suddenly...<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"I want to tell her the feelings I have are Cal’s not mine. But if I did it would be a white lie. There are a lot of reasons I have feelings for the woman in those pictures...<br><br>And Cal isn’t one of them."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381095904ra/4179743.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really loved Lauren and Chris together. The way that they're shy around one another is so cute, and I just absolutely adore their chemistry. I love how Chris is so sweet towards Lauren, and how at the end, he just can't deny that Lauren has managed to get to his system.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"The three things I like about Cal are: he met you, he made Caylen and he brought you both into my life."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>And <b>OMG</b> the sexual tension between them is so frustrating.<br><i>
  <blockquote>"It’s taking everything in me to keep my arms at my sides. Every ounce of determination I have is being employed to, stamp out the urge to wrap my arms around the small of her back, pulling her against me and kissing her lips that are barely open but begging me to taste them."</blockquote>
</i> <br>But then that ending...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395928427ra/9063298.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, I definitely need the next installment! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Because I loved him, and I still had hope.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418035558ra/12648293.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, 5 stars to this book!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="872231941344692193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

This author's voice was powerful enough to convey what it feels like when you cannot trust yourself and live in a perpetual state of fear.<br><br>I liked Chris in the novella but I admit I was losing patience with him in this book, his mental instability was painful to read about because it seemed too real. Lauren was her usual amazing self but she was sometimes too kind with her husband ;) !!<br><br>The plot seems to thicken around what triggers Cal to appear &amp; disappear... The family dynamics between Chris &amp; his parents was interesting and explains a lot about him. I am not sure I understand what the hell the fake fiancée is still doing here &amp; I am tired of Chris BEING A PUSHOVER... <br><br>The ending was frustratingly perfect though !! I was breathless &amp; giddy LOL now I need to bother Portia Moore to know when the next gem is being published because HOW CAN I WAIT ANY LONGER?<br><br>If you have any doubt YES I recommend this book but read them in order &amp; you'll have one fun roller coaster ride :)<br>cheers</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14422625053293783352">I only gave this book four stars because of poor editing/proof reading. In my copy there were a lot of grammatical errors which I do find very, very annoying.<br/><br/>Having said that I found the storyline excellent, so different from your usually virgin meets billionaire, angst ridden crap that is around a lot these days. It was very emotional, the main characters were great and the support characters were more than one dimensional. It was a good story, well told, and the cliffhanger ending was perfect.</span>
  <span id="freeText14422625053293783352" style="display:none">I only gave this book four stars because of poor editing/proof reading. In my copy there were a lot of grammatical errors which I do find very, very annoying.<br /><br />Having said that I found the storyline excellent, so different from your usually virgin meets billionaire, angst ridden crap that is around a lot these days. It was very emotional, the main characters were great and the support characters were more than one dimensional. It was a good story, well told, and the cliffhanger ending was perfect.<br /><br />I'm looking forward to the final book which has to give Lauren a happy ending because she is the only one who loves and can cope with both Chris and Cal.</span>

  <span id="freeText13644617441111840363" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Mashocist-of-Love stars...</b><br><br>This series got me hooked! And I enjoyed reading them so much. Uh, not really... I mean, im not happy when Lauren hurt. :(<br><br>In this book, this is where Lauren...put herself..to be a MASOCHIST...for the sake of her dear lovely Caylen...<br><br>Apparently people will do anything for their little one. No matter how it'll make them feel and whatever they must bear...<br><br>There were times when I hoped she just moved on with her life... Date other guys.. SCREW THE SCOTTS!! It's okay to be a bitch sometimes.<br><br>Good thing that she has best friends like Angela &amp; Hillary and her aunt Raven. Although, Hillary is bitchy sometimes but that's her unique. I loved her bitch side especially at the incident with the MEGA BITCH Jenna. My favorites of Hillary on Lauren..<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Look, I'm sorry to disrespect your house like that. I told your mom, so now I'm telling you. For that, I apologize." she says, throwing her hands up. "But I'm not going to let anyone talk to my best friend that way, especially when she's trying to be nice."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><i>"How long have you guys been friends?" Lisa asks cautiously.</i><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Since college. We're not on the best terms right now, but I'll be damned if I let someone talk to her like that." She then turns her attention to me.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>"At first I thought you were lying. I didn't know whether to believe all this or not, but now I know you're not Cal," she says, looking at me bitterly.<br><br>I sigh. "Why is that?" I ask</blockquote>
</i><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Cal would never let anyone to talk to Lauren like that."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Hillary, I'm so proud of you!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430195688ra/14691070.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When reading this, sometimes I think the story feels like a joke of Lauren's life. No offense. And I can't help but thinking: What if the author was Alessandra Torre? I bet she will fuck my mind more than this author did to me. <br><br>TBH, this story has potential to fuck our mind more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22471294.Black_Lies" title="Black Lies by Alessandra Torre" rel="nofollow noopener">Black Lies</a> has done. But for that case, BL still won the mind-fucking game. <br><br>STILL, the ending got me<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430195688ra/14691071.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1107271277" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1107271277" />
    <a title="Daphne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28000534-daphne"><img alt="Daphne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589448083p2/28000534.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107271277?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daphne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daphne" href="/user/show/28000534-daphne">Daphne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=all-time-faves">all-time-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=must-read-2014">must-read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=sequels-i-kill-for">sequels-i-kill-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=omfg-cliffhanger-much">omfg-cliffhanger-much</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=awesome-heroines">awesome-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=possessive-caveman-cuties">possessive-caveman-cuties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28000534-daphne?shelf=green-eyed-heroes">green-eyed-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107271277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4049802829304451640">It's just a four for me. Why? Because of that damn cliffhanger. I know those who read this will understand my feelings. Okay, maybe a 4.5 since I just damn love Chris and Cal.<br/><br/>I became obsessed with this series when I read the first book which made me cry like a major baby by the way. I can't believe I let a day pass by and didn't read this on the day it was published. <br/>Oh, now I remember. There was a delay and the fact that I live in another country didn't help with the timezone. When it went liv</span>
  <span id="freeText4049802829304451640" style="display:none">It's just a four for me. Why? Because of that damn cliffhanger. I know those who read this will understand my feelings. Okay, maybe a 4.5 since I just damn love Chris and Cal.<br /><br />I became obsessed with this series when I read the first book which made me cry like a major baby by the way. I can't believe I let a day pass by and didn't read this on the day it was published. <br />Oh, now I remember. There was a delay and the fact that I live in another country didn't help with the timezone. When it went live, I was probably close to sleeping and reading another book.<br />Anyway, as soon as I got it last night, I told myself that I was going to read this as soon as I finish the book that I was reading. I started reading this around 12:30 am and finished around 4 am. I'm a very dedicated reader when it comes to this book.<br /><br />I liked hearing from Chris's point of view. In fact, I sort of hoped for one when I read the novella. It was refreshing having an idea what he was feeling. I honestly kept wondering why in the world he's so head over heels in love with a puppy kicker then I think about Lauren and wonder why she's with Cal anyway. <br /><br />But unlike Jenna (Chris's fiance), Cal had redeeming qualities that I actually liked. Cal came across as cold, indifferent and arrogant in the first book and I hated he acted like a jerk towards Lauren but I now understand why he's like that. His redeeming qualities would probably include that he fights for Lauren. He would never let anyone talk down to her the way Jenna and Chris's father does. Chris tries his best to steer their attention away from Lauren and often scolds them but come on! I like imagining how Cal would react and he'd probably yell at them or shove them out of the house. Better yet, he and Lauren should walk out!<br />Let's not also forget the fact that even if he disappears for a huge amount of time, he always comes back for Lauren. He always fights for them and that's why I love him. <br /><br />Chris on the other hand is the polar opposite of Cal. He's sweet, caring, kind and attentive. He obviously adores their daughter Caylen and cares for Lauren. Whether as a friend or more, he doesn't know. He's confused a lot in this book. He's also very stressed out and not like the laid back, happy go lucky guy that some of the characters described. Well, there is a reason why he is like that anyway.<br /><br />Now Lauren. I liked Lauren in the first book. She says what's on her mind with little hesitation and it often got her in tight situations with Cal but here... She held back. Sure, she still tells Chris stuff but not as much. She doesn't comment on the fact that whenever they're having a nice time that someone (Usually Jenna or William aka his father) ruins it. She doesn't say anything when he involuntarily hurts her. Oh he knows what he's doing but he still does it anyway.<br /><br />I didn't like the fact that Chris juggled his feelings with Jenna and Lauren in this book as well. A lot of people in the book told him to choose one to focus his attention on because people shouldn't have to remind themselves that they love this person. But Chris being Chris does it anyway.<br /><br />Reading this book, I have developed a theory that Cal might have more control than Chris does. He controls when he comes and goes, when he shows memories and I'm pretty sure if he chose to take over, he can probably do it. Now that I think about it, as much as I love Chris, I'll probably choose Cal over him. Mostly because Cal acts on his feelings and not like Chris who hides them.<br /><br />All in all, I loved it. I didn't cry at all and I pretty much expected to bawl my eyes out. Except I didn't and I wished I did. I like crying over these characters. <br /><br />Can't wait for Spring 2015 although I need a title and an exact date to satisfy myself. :) </span>
  <a data-text-id="4049802829304451640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1541713408" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1541713408" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1541713408?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1541713408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15546035028098729126"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382766162i/6182035.png' width='190' height='119' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><b>Stay connected with my reviews, book news and more: <br/><a href='http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Blog- Jessica’s Book Review</a> | <a href='https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> | <a href='https://www.twitter.com/jessbookreview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> </b> <br/> <br/>So if you are reading this, you read the first book in the series. I hope so! I do not want to ruin anything for you :) This will be a pretty simple review, as I do not want to ruin anything for you as the reader. <br/><br/>At the end of book one, Cal tells Lauren has to leave and he will not be coming back. She assumes he is leaving her, possibly even for another woman. He promises her that is not the </span>
  <span id="freeText15546035028098729126" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382766162i/6182035.png" width="190" height="119" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>Stay connected with my reviews, book news and more: <br><a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog- Jessica’s Book Review</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/jessbookreview" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> </b> <br> <br>So if you are reading this, you read the first book in the series. I hope so! I do not want to ruin anything for you :) This will be a pretty simple review, as I do not want to ruin anything for you as the reader. <br><br>At the end of book one, Cal tells Lauren has to leave and he will not be coming back. She assumes he is leaving her, possibly even for another woman. He promises her that is not the case but she doesn't believe anything he tells her anymore. When he leaves, Lauren finds out she is pregnant and has to be strong for their child. That is where book 2 in the series begins. Lauren is celebrating their daughter's first birthday with friends and family. She hasn't moved on from Cal but she is starting to feel like maybe she can. Things seem to be going better when she learns where Cal is. Lauren goes after him, not for her but for their child. What she discovers... oh my, what she discovers will knock your socks off!!! <br><br>Portia Moore did it again. She had me at every page, every word. I couldn't wait to finish the page I was reading so fast just to find what happens next. I could not believe what I was reading. I felt so torn for them all and Lauren, poor Lauren! I also loved the dual POV's. It was essential to hear from both characters. I can't imagine only reading from Lauren's POV. It would have driven me crazy not knowing what "he" thinks and feels. <br><br>I ended up falling in love with Chris. They are both so different, yet the same. Lauren really deserves to be happy, but in this situation can she truly be? This was a real page-turner. I couldn't put the book down. I was even cooking dinner over the stove not able to put down my Kindle. I am sad, yet excited to read the next and last book of the trilogy. I just hope Lauren, Chris, and even Cal will get their HEA. There was so much damage and no one to trust. They all deserve peace and resolution. <br> <br>I give Almost Broken (If I Break #2) 4.5 Stars!<br><br>P.S. My advice to you, have book 3 ready to go! You will WANT it ASAP! </span>
  <a data-text-id="15546035028098729126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34388652-x1f339-natasha-x1f339?shelf=books-on-my-kindle">books-on-my-kindle</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer10825064244086646914">Ok here I go and there will probably be spoilers so if you haven't read any of these books then I suggest not reading any further. <br/><br/>When I read the first book in this series I'll admit I wasn't thrilled about it. I honestly didn't think that it could get better so I sat here for a couple of days wondering if I should even continue. Well after I introduced the book to my cousin, she continued on to read the next 2 and said that they were getting really good. That's when I thought to myself, "Well </span>
  <span id="freeText10825064244086646914" style="display:none">Ok here I go and there will probably be spoilers so if you haven't read any of these books then I suggest not reading any further. <br /><br />When I read the first book in this series I'll admit I wasn't thrilled about it. I honestly didn't think that it could get better so I sat here for a couple of days wondering if I should even continue. Well after I introduced the book to my cousin, she continued on to read the next 2 and said that they were getting really good. That's when I thought to myself, "Well I've already started and I do want to see what happens." So I continued and boy am I glad I did. I said I was going to give Portia Moore another chance to change my mind and she did. <br /><br />I don't know about anyone else but I'm actually infatuated with Cal! There's something just so sexy about him and I want more! The entire book I kept waiting and waiting for him to come back. Now I like Chris but I did not like the way he kept bashing Cal. Cal is a part of him and he needs to accept that! I feel incredibly sorry for Lauren! Not only has she been through enough with all these secrets and lies but now she has to deal with Mr. Scott and the ever so annoying Jenna who by the way I hope drives off a cliff! Maybe her and Mr. Scott can take that drive together:) <br /><br />When I read that last line of the book, I couldn't help but smile but I'm not happy that we have to wait until the Spring of 2015 to see what happens! I've been wanting Cal to come back this entire time and the fact that he does or at least it feels like it's him at the end has got me screaming! These characters are unique and after reading these last 2 books it really gave me a better understanding of the first book! It changed my whole perspective and I can honestly say that the review I gave the first one is definitely worth more than the 2 I gave it! So Portia, thank you for writing a great story and I cannot wait to continue on! </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1113270174" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3540726800314401907">I just finished this book and I literally had to walk outside and take a deep breath! Did it really just end that way? Right when things were finally getting exciting!<br/><br/>My cousin introduced me to this series and I am extremely grateful! The characters felt real, like they were people I actually know or have met before. Lauren is amazing. I couldn't stand her in the first book. She honestly just seemed like a complete "puppy kicker" to me. But after really getting to know her, she turned out be an </span>
  <span id="freeText3540726800314401907" style="display:none">I just finished this book and I literally had to walk outside and take a deep breath! Did it really just end that way? Right when things were finally getting exciting!<br /><br />My cousin introduced me to this series and I am extremely grateful! The characters felt real, like they were people I actually know or have met before. Lauren is amazing. I couldn't stand her in the first book. She honestly just seemed like a complete "puppy kicker" to me. But after really getting to know her, she turned out be an amazing and strong woman. I couldn't imagine going through any of what she goes through in these books. And Cal.....oh Cal! He's such an arrogant ass.....but definitely the bad guy that most girls want. I was able to read this book in less than a day in its entirety. I thought this was the last one, so I was devastated when it just ended with a cliffhanger like it did. It was an amazing way to end, but.....I can't believe we have to wait til spring to finally find out what happens next!! I really hope Lauren and Caylen get the happy ending they deserve. #TeamCal #TeamLauren</span>
  <a data-text-id="3540726800314401907" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sD0wVPZ+DBHtlqE0HeuLBKrN9NgzZQ74uzoGQy/ja+qrZ3uY3zf0TIFfOq958ZJs8iDQTKUlR6n56CQiFYXRDQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('K1EqyPQFQQ+9HY9hcu5OvwgM6p1Z7bFyzmH5cyHA8rswC2EE3Uy5UtHUFPoW9FfXUOHOCc+t+COMs9sSG6ZIXA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
